<script>
	// Create a loading framework for external JavaScript (contained in eSpots)
	function loadScript(url, callback){

	    var script = document.createElement("script")
	    script.type = "text/javascript";
	    script.async = true;
	    if (script.readyState){  //IE
	        script.onreadystatechange = function(){
	            if (script.readyState == "complete"){
	                script.onreadystatechange = null;
	                callback();
	            }
	        };
	    } else {  //Others
	        script.onload = function(){
	            callback();
	        };
	    }
	    script.src = url;
	    // For non compliant html5 support (IE8/WindowsXP) issue, insert into Head
	    document.head = document.head || document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
	    document.head.appendChild(script);
	}
</script>

<div data-analytics="center-middle" class="genericESpot" id="WC_ContentAreaESpot_div_1_52701" style="width: 950px; min-height: -1px;">
	
	    <p class="caption" style="display:none" id="WC_ContentAreaESpot_div_2_52701">[FOOTER_All_Content_2]</p>   
	
            <div class="ad" id="ad_52701">
        <script type="text/javascript">

// Catalogue eSpot Tag v2.14 26-Nov-15
//

(function (active) {
    var analytics = {
        d: {},
        log: function (message, o) {
            window.console && console.log('eSpot analytics: ', message, (o == undefined ? '' : o));
        },
        ga_initialised: false,
        ga: function (d) {
            var opts = {}, c_opts = {}, event_only = false;
            var pd = d.product_details ? '|PRODUCT_DETAILS' : '';

 			if (d.user_id) {
 				c_opts['userId'] = d.user_id;
 				opts['dimension19'] = d.user_id;
 				opts['dimension9'] = 'Logged On';
 			}
 			else{
 				opts['dimension9'] = 'Logged Off';
 			}
				
			if (!analytics.ga_initalised) {
				ga('create', 'UA-29884571-2', (location.hostname.match(/coles\.com\.au$/i)==null ? '' : 'coles.com.au'), c_opts);
				ga('require', 'displayfeatures');
				ga('require', 'ec', 'ec.js');
				analytics.ga_initalised = true;
			}
			
            if (d.page)
                opts['page'] = d.page;

			if (d.cl=='New'){
                opts['dimension12'] = 0;
                opts['dimension14'] = 'New';
			}
			
			if (d.cl=='Experienced'){
				opts['dimension14'] = 'Experienced';
			}
			            
            if (d.localisation) {
                ga('send', 'event', 'Localisation', d.localisation, location.pathname);
            }
            
            // Set product sort custom dimension
            if (d.sort_by){
            	opts['dimension15'] = d.sort_by;
            }
            
            // Set auto search suggest event
            if (d.search_terms && d.search_method){
            	ga('send', 'event', 'Search', d.search_method, d.search_terms.join('|'));
            }
            
            // DSS tracking
            if (d.event && d.event.match(/ds_selected|ds_changed/)){
            	var ea = d.event=='ds_selected' ? '-Selected' : '-Changed';
            	var el = d.day_of_week+'|'+d.time_slot+(d.restriction ? '|R:'+d.restriction : '');
            	ga('send', 'event', 'DSS', d.dss_viewed+ea, el);
            	event_only = true;
            } else if (d.dss_viewed) {
            	ga('send', 'event', 'DSS', d.dss_viewed+'-Viewed', (d.restriction ? 'R:'+d.restriction : ''));
			}
			
			// Internal Campaign Click Tracking
            if (d.int_campaign_c) {
				ga('ec:addPromo', {
					'id': d.int_campaign_c,
					'name': d.int_campaign_c,
					'creative': '',
					'position': d.catalog ? d.catalog : ''
				});
				ga('ec:setAction', 'promo_click');
                ga('send', 'event', 'Internal Promotion', 'Click', d.catalog ? d.catalog : '');
//                 if (!d.inline)
//                 	event_only = true;
			}

 			// Internal Campaign Impression Tracking
			if (d.int_campaign_i) {
				dojo.forEach(d.int_campaign_i, function (e) {
					ga('ec:addPromo', {
						'id': e['name'],
						'name': e['name'],
						'creative': '',
						'position': e['pos']
					});
				});
            }
            
            // Custom dimensions
            if (d.cust) {
				var labels = ['cust', 'state', 'region', null, 'fcntr', 'flybuys'];
				for (i = 0; i < labels.length; i++) {
					if (labels[i])
						opts['dimension' + (i + 3)] = d[labels[i]];
				}
			}
			            
            if (d.registration_event) {
                ga('send', 'event', 'Registration', d.registration_event, opts);
                opts['page'] = '/register/success/' + d.registration_event
            }

            if (d.login_event)
                ga('send', 'event', 'Log In', d.login_event, opts);

            // External campaign tracking via WT.mc_id   
            if (d.ext_campaign_id) {
                var c = d.ext_campaign_id.split('_');
                var ga_cd = ['campaignName', 'campaignMedium', 'campaignSource', 'campaignContent', 'campaignKeyword'];
                dojo.forEach(d.ext_campaign_id.split('_'), function (v, i) {
                    ga('set', ga_cd[i], v);
                });
                ga('set', 'campaignId', d.ext_campaign_id);
            }

            // Product Details View
            if (d.product_details) {
	            ga('ec:addProduct', d.product_details);
				ga('ec:setAction', 'detail');
            }

            // Javascript Exception Tracking
            if (d.exception) {
                ga('send', 'event', 'JavaScript', 'Analytics eSpot Exception', d.exception);
                event_only = true;
            }
            
            // Aisle/Search Tracking
            if (d.catalog)
                opts['dimension11'] = d.catalog.replace(/_/g, ' > ');

            // Product Tracking
            if(d.products){
            	var products = d.products[0];
				limit = 0;
				for(i in products) {
					var p = products[i];
					limit++;
					if (limit<41) {
						ga('ec:addImpression', {
							'id': p['sku'],
							'name': p['name'],
							'brand': p['brand'],
							'position': p['position'],
							'list': (d.int_campaign_c ? d.int_campaign_c+pd : p.category)
						});
					}
				}
				if (d.event && d.event.match(/upsell_page_view/)) {
					event_only = true;
					ga('send', 'event', 'Product Promotion', 'Impression', 'Upsell', opts);
				}
            }

			// Add to Cart
			if (d.event && d.event.match(/add-to-cart|add-to-trolley/)) {
				var label = '', value = 0, s_type = 'None';
				if (d.catalog) {
					ga('set', {'dimension11': d.catalog.replace(/_/g, ' > '), 'metric2': 1});			
					label = 'List';
					value = d.rank;
				}

				if (d.promo) {
					ga('ec:addProduct',{ 
						'id': d.promo['sku'], 
						'name': d.promo['name'], 
						'brand': d.promo['brand'],
						'position':d.promo['position']
					});
					ga('ec:setAction', 'add', {'list': d.int_campaign_c ? d.int_campaign_c+pd : d.promo.category});
					label = d.promo.category && d.promo.category.match(/\|List/i) ? label : 'Promotion';
					s_type = analytics.utils.price_promo(d.promo);
				}
				if (d.product_details) 
					label = 'Product Details';
				if (d.search) 
					label = 'Search';
				if (d.my_usuals)
					label = 'My Usuals';
				if (d.my_orders)
					label = 'My Orders';	
				ga('send', 'event', 'Add to Trolley', label, s_type, value);
				event_only = true;
			}
			
			// Refunds
			if (d.refund) {
				ga('ec:setAction', 'refund', {'id': d.refund});				
				ga('send', 'event', 'Order', d.operation, d.reason);
				event_only = true;
			}
			
			// Check if user seen the spend stretch banner
			if (d.offer){
				opts['dimension20'] = d.offer;
			}

            if (!event_only) {
            	if (location.href.match(/[a-zA-Z0-9_.+-]+(@|%40)[a-zA-Z0-9-]+\.[a-zA-Z0-9-.]+/i)){
            		opts['page'] = location.pathname;
            	}	
	  	 		ga('send', 'pageview', opts);
	  	 	} 
        },
		aa_initialised: false,
		aa_loaded: false,
		aa: function(d){
			var s=window.s, event_only=false, events=[];			

			if (!analytics.aa_initalised) {
				s.account = location.hostname=='shop.coles.com.au' ? 'colesonline-prod' : 'colesonline-dev';
				s.channel  = 'Desktop';
				s.eVar22 = s.channel;
				s.campaign = d.ext_campaign_id;
				s.server = window.location.hostname;
				s.trackInlineStats = true;
				analytics.aa_initalised = true;
				

				// Page name and hierarchies
				var h = ['col', 'desktop'].concat(d.section);
				s.hier1 	= h.join('|').toLowerCase();
				s.pageName 	= h.join(':').toLowerCase();
				s.prop1		= d.section[0];	

				// Internal Campaign Impression Tracking
				if (d.int_campaign_i) {
					var ip=[];
					dojo.forEach(d.int_campaign_i, function (e) {
						ip.push(e.name);
					});
					if (ip.length>0) {
						s.list1 = ip.join(';');
						events.push('event1');
					}
				}

				// Internal Campaign Click Tracking
				if (d.int_campaign_c) {
					s.list1 = d.int_campaign_c;
					s.eVar18 = d.int_campaign_c;
					events.push('event2');
					events.push('event32')
				}
				
				if (d.dss_viewed) {
					events.push('event21');
					events.push('event22');
					s.eVar23 = d.dss_viewed;
					if (d.restriction && d.restriction !=''){
						events.push('event27');
						if (d.restriction.match(/Liquor/i))
							events.push('event28');
						if (d.restriction.match(/Tobacco/i))
							events.push('event29');
					}
				}				
			}
			
			if (d.user_id) 
				s.eVar30 = d.user_id;

			if (d.cl=='New'){
				s.eVar11 = '0';
				s.eVar12 = 'New';
			}
		
			if (d.cl=='Experienced'){
				s.eVar12 = 'Experienced';
			}
			
			// Customer dimensions
			if (d.cust) {
				var labels = ['fcntr', 'state', 'region', 'cust'];
				for (i = 0; i < labels.length; i++) {
					if (labels[i])
						s['eVar' + (i + 4)] = d[labels[i]];
				}
				s.eVar90 = d.flybuys ? d.flybuys : '';
			}
			
			if (d.postcode){
				s.eVar8 = d.postcode;
			}

			// Login status
			if (d.user_id){
				s.eVar89 = 'Logged On';
			} else{
				s.eVar89 = 'Logged Off';
			}
			
			// Localisation	
			if (d.localisation) {
				events.push('event14');
				events.push('event18');
			}

            if (d.registration_event){
				events.push('event4');
				events.push('event17');	  
			}
			
            if (d.login_event){
				s.eVar13 = d.login_event;
				events.push('event3');
				events.push('event16');
			}
			
			if (d.search_terms && d.search_method){            	
            	s.eVar38 = d.search_method;
            	s.eVar37 = d.search_terms[1];
            	s.eVar36 = d.search_terms[2];
            	s.eVar82 = d.search_terms[0];
            	events.push('event41');
            }
            
            // search workflow
            if ((d.preceding_search && d.search_method && d.search_result==undefined) || (d.preceding_search && d.search_result=='no_results')){
            		events.push('event43');
            }
            
            if (d.search_result && d.search_result.match(/no_results/i)){
            	events.push('event44');
            }	  

			// DSS Slot Selected or Changed				
			if (d.event && d.event.match(/ds_selected|ds_changed/)) {
				events.push(d.event=='ds_selected' ? 'event23' : 'event25');
				events.push(d.event=='ds_selected' ? 'event24' : 'event26');
				s.eVar23 = d.context;
				
				s.eVar24 = d.method;
				s.eVar25 = d.day_of_week;
				s.eVar26 = d.time_slot;
				s.eVar27 = d.delivery_date;
				s.eVar28 = d.days_to_delivery
				
				if (d.restriction && d.restriction !=''){
					events.push('event27');
					if (d.restriction.match(/Liquor/i))
						events.push('event28');
					if (d.restriction.match(/Tobacco/i))
						events.push('event29');
				}
				
				if (d.cost !=''){
					events.push('event30='+d.cost);
				}
				
			}
			
			// Order cancellation
			if (d.order && d.operation && d.operation=='Cancelled'){
				var order_id = d.refund.split('-')[0];
				events.push('event49:'+d.order.id); 
				s.eVar31 = d.refund;
				s.eVar32 = order_id;
			}
			
			//modify order - start
			if (d.order && d.operation && d.operation=='Modified'){
				var id_mc 	= d.order.id+'-'+d.order.mod_count;
				s.eVar31 = id_mc;
				s.eVar32 = d.order.id;

				if (d.order.skus) {
					var products = [];
					var sk 		= d.order.skus.split(';');
					var up 		= d.order.prices.split(';');
					var qn 		= d.order.quantities.split(';');
					var bv		= 0;
					dojo.forEach(sk, function(sku, i){
						products.push(';'+sku+';'+qn[i]+';'+up[i]+';event65='+up[i]+'|event63='+qn[i]);
						bv += Number(up[i]);
					});
				
					s.products = products.join(',');
					events.push('event57='+bv+':'+id_mc);
				}
				events.push('event56:'+id_mc);
				events.push('event65:'+id_mc);
				events.push('event63:'+id_mc);
			}	
			
			
            // Product Impression Tracking
            if (d.products) {
	            var products = d.products[0];
				var aa_products = [];
				var s_type = '';
				for(i in products) {
					var p = products[i];
					if (p.location) {
						var eVars=[];
						eVars.push('eVar1='+p.location);
						eVars.push('eVar2='+p.feature_spot);
						if (p.position)
							eVars.push('eVar3='+p.position);
						if (d.int_campaign_c)
							eVars.push('eVar33='+d.int_campaign_c);
						if (d.aisle)	
							eVars.push('eVar40='+d.aisle.join('_'));
						if (d.search_terms){ 
							eVars.push('eVar35='+d.search_terms[0]);
						}
						s_type = analytics.utils.price_promo(p);
            			eVars.push('eVar41='+s_type);
						aa_products.push(';'+p.sku+';;;;'+eVars.join('|'));
					}
				}
				if (aa_products.length>0) {
					s.products = aa_products.join(',');
					events.push('event5');
					events.push('event6='+aa_products.length);
					
					if (d.product_details){
						events.push('event60');
					}

					if (d.event && d.event.match(/page_load|onclicking_Tab/)) {
						event_only = true;
						s.linkTrackVars = 'products';
						s.linkTrackEvents = 'event5';
						s.tl();
					}
				}
            }
            
			// Add to cart
			if (d.event && d.event.match(/add-to-cart/)) {
				var section = '', s_type='', events=[], lt_vars=['channel', 'prop1', 'eVar22'];
				if (d.promo) {
					var product_evars = [
						'eVar1='	+d.promo.location,
						'eVar19='	+d.promo.location,
						'eVar2='	+d.promo.feature_spot,
						'eVar20='	+d.promo.feature_spot
					];
					if (d.promo.position) {
						product_evars.push('eVar3='+d.promo.position);
						product_evars.push('eVar21='+d.promo.position);
						events.push('event45='+d.promo.position);
					}
					if (d.int_campaign_c) {
						product_evars.push('eVar33='+d.int_campaign_c);
						product_evars.push('eVar34='+d.int_campaign_c);
					}
					if (d.aisle) {
						product_evars.push('eVar10='+d.aisle.join('_'));
						product_evars.push('eVar40='+d.aisle.join('_'));
					}
					if (d.search_terms) {
            			product_evars.push('eVar35='+d.search_terms[0]);
            			product_evars.push('eVar39='+d.search_terms[0]);
            		}
            		s_type = analytics.utils.price_promo(d.promo);
            		product_evars.push('eVar41='+s_type);
            		product_evars.push('eVar42='+s_type);
            		
					s.products = ';'+d.promo.sku+';;;;'+product_evars.join('|');
					lt_vars.push('products');
				}
									
				if (d.search_result=='success'){
					events.push('event42');	
				}
				
				events.push('event7');
				events.push('event15');
				
				
				s.events = events.join(',');
				s.linkTrackVars = lt_vars.join(',');	
				s.linkTrackEvents = events.join(',').replace(/=\d+/, '');
				s.tl(true,'o','Add to Trolley');
				event_only = true;	
			}      
            
 			if (!event_only) {
 				s.events = events.join(',');
 				s.t();
 			}
		},
		tracking_beacon: function(src){
			var b = document.createElement('img');
			b.src = src;
			b.style.cssText = 'width:1px; height:1px; border:0px; display:none'; 
			document.body.appendChild(b);
		},
        mm: function(d){
        	var id, adid, send_data=false;
        	if (d.homepage) {
        		id = '502757';
        		adid = '125283';
        		send_data = true;
        	}
        	
        	if (d.registration_event) {
        		id = '689942';
        		adid = '125283';
        		send_data = true;
        	}
        	
        	if (send_data) {
				var img = new Image(1, 1);
				img.src = '//pixel.mathtag.com/event/img?mt_id='+id+'&mt_adid='+adid+'&v1=&v2=&v3=&s1=&s2=&s3='
			}
        },
        aw: function(d){
            if (d.registration_event || d.login_event) {
				require(["dojo/io/script"], function(script){
					var deferred = script.get({'url': '//www.googleadservices.com/pagead/conversion_async.js'});
					deferred.then(function(){
						window.google_trackConversion({
						  google_conversion_id: 1066356933, 
						  google_custom_params: {},
						  google_remarketing_only: true
						});				
					});
				});
			}
        },
        tw: function(d){
        	var send_data=[];
        
			if (d.homepage) {
				send_data.push({'tracking_id':'l6lx8', 'bv': 0, 'oq': 0});
			}
			if (d.registration_event){
				send_data.push({'tracking_id':'l6lx6', 'bv': 0, 'oq': 0});
			}
			if(d.login_event){
				send_data.push({'tracking_id':'l6lx7', 'bv': 0, 'oq': 0});
			}
			
			dojo.forEach(send_data, function(p){
				analytics.tracking_beacon('https://analytics.twitter.com/i/adsct?txn_id='+p.tracking_id+'&p_id=Twitter&tw_sale_amount='+p.bv+'&tw_order_quantity='+p.oq);
				analytics.tracking_beacon('//t.co/i/adsct?txn_id='+p.tracking_id+'&p_id=Twitter&tw_sale_amount='+p.bv+'&tw_order_quantity='+p.oq);
			});	
        },
        si: function(d){
        	var codes = {'PRODL':	'si-7-12', 
        				'PRODS':	'si-7-48',
        				'SVTL': 	'si-7-47',
        				'SVTS':		'si-7-43',
        				'SITL': 	'si-7-45',
        				'SIT': 		'si-7-42',
        				'DEV': 		'si-7-10'};
			window.Process180.GetSurveyInitiator(codes[d.env] ? codes[d.env] : 'si-7-12');
        },
        track: function (d) {
			analytics.aa_loaded.then(function(){analytics.aa(d)});
            analytics.ga(d);
 			analytics.mm(d); 
 			analytics.aw(d);
 			analytics.tw(d); 
        },
        utils: {
            order: {
            	window:	14, // days before old order data is removed
            	set: function(id, order){
            		localStorage['order_'+id] = JSON.stringify({
            			order: 		order,
            			date: 		Date.now()
            		});
            	},
            	get: function(id){
            		var order = localStorage['order_'+id];
            		return(order ? JSON.parse(order) : order);
            	},
            	tidy: function(){
            		for(k in localStorage) {
            			if (k.match(/^order_/)) {
            				var order = JSON.parse(localStorage[k]);
            				if (Date.now()-order.date > window*86400000)
            					localStorage.removeItem(k);
            			}
            		}
            	},
            	remove: function(id){
            		localStorage.removeItem('order_'+id);
            	}
            },
            format_promo: function(promo, presentation){
            	if (presentation) {
	    			return(['Upsell Page_' + promo['category'] + '_' + presentation, promo['promotion'], promo['sku'] + '-' + promo['brand'] + '-' + promo['name']]);
	    		} else {
					return([promo['category'], promo['sku'] + '-' + promo['name']]);
				}
			},
			get_parameter: function(parameter){
				var value = location.search.match(new RegExp(parameter+'=([^$&]*)'));
				return value && value.length==2 ? value[1] : '';
			},
			clean_upsell_dl: function(d) {
				var clean_dl = {};
				if (d.event=='add-to-trolley') {
					clean_dl.event = 'add-to-cart';
					for(p in d.promo) {
						if (p.match(/^catEntry_/)) {
							clean_dl.promo = {
								location: 'Upsell Page',
								feature_spot: d.promo[p].promotion,
								sku: d.promo[p].sku,
								name: d.promo[p].name,
								brand: d.promo[p].brand,
								category: 'Upsell Page_'+d.promo[p].category+'_page'
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if (d.event.match(/page_load|onclicking_Tab/)) {
					clean_dl = {event: 'upsell_page_view', presentation: 'page', products: [{}]};
					for(p in d.promo) {
						if (p.match(/^catEntry_/)) {
							clean_dl.products[0][p] = {
								location: 'Upsell Page',
								feature_spot: d.promo[p].promotion,
								sku: d.promo[p].sku,
								name: d.promo[p].name,
								brand: d.promo[p].brand,
								category: 'Upsell Page_'+d.promo[p].category+'_page'
							}					
						}
					}
				}
				return(clean_dl);
			},
			my_order_list: function(products, d){
				var position = 0;
				dojo.query('div.product-box').forEach(function(item) {
						position++
			
							if (item.getAttribute('data-refresh').match(/partNumber:\s*"(\d+)/m).length>0) {
						
								var p_sku 			= item.getAttribute('data-refresh').match(/partNumber:\s*"(\d+)/m)[1];
								var cat_entry_id 	= 'catEntry_' + item.getAttribute('data-refresh').match(/catEntryId:\s*"(\d+)/m)[1];
								var links 			= dojo.query('div.detail a.product-url', item);
								var class_name		= item.className;
								var promotion = (class_name && class_name.match(/promo/)) ? true : false;
								links = (links.length != 0) ? links : dojo.query('div.productTitle a.accessibility', item)
								var p_name 			= links[0].href.match(/[^$\/]+$/)[0];
		
								products[cat_entry_id] = {
									location: d.location,
									feature_spot: d.placement,
									term_aisle: d.aisle ? d.aisle.join('_') : (d.search_terms ? d.search_terms[0] : ''),
									category: d.category,
									sku: p_sku,
									name: p_name,
									promotion: promotion,
									position: position,
									s_type: class_name
								};
							};
				});
				return(products);
			},		
			special_case: function(response_dom, args, d){
				var position = 0;
				dojo.query('div.prodtile > form', response_dom).forEach(function(item) {
					position++
					dojo.query('div[data-refresh]', item).forEach(function (node) {
						if (node.getAttribute('data-refresh').match(/partNumber:\s*"(\d+)/m).length>0) {
						
							var p_sku 			= node.getAttribute('data-refresh').match(/partNumber:\s*"(\d+)/m)[1];
							var cat_entry_id 	= 'catEntry_' + node.getAttribute('data-refresh').match(/catEntryId:\s*"(\d+)/m)[1];
							var links 			= dojo.query('div.detail a.product-url', node);
							var class_name		= node.className;
							var promotion = (class_name && class_name.match(/promo/)) ? true : false;
							links = (links.length != 0) ? links : dojo.query('div.productTitle a.accessibility', node)
							var p_name 			= links[0].href.match(/[^$\/]+$/)[0];
		
							args.promos[cat_entry_id] = {
								location: d.location,
								feature_spot: d.placement,
								term_aisle: d.aisle ? d.aisle.join('_') : (d.search_terms ? d.search_terms[0] : ''),
								category: d.category,
								sku: p_sku,
								name: p_name,
								promotion: promotion,
								position: position,
								s_type: class_name
							};
						};
					});
				});
				return(args.promos);
			},
			price_promo: function(product){
				var s_type = 'None';
				s_type = (product.s_type && product.s_type.match(/promo/)) ? product.s_type.replace(/(promo|-)/g, ' ').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '') : s_type;
				s_type = s_type=='save' ? 'Specials' : s_type.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + s_type.slice(1);
				return s_type;
			}
        },
        rules: function (d, query, topic) {
        	
        	// Get Environment
        	dojo.query('input[name="environmentKey"]').forEach(function(e){
        		d.env = e.value;
        	});

    		//  Detect Localisation Event
    		wtc = dojo.cookie('onLoadWebtrendsCookie');
    		if (wtc) {
    			// Detect localisation event
    			le = wtc.match(/WT.z_lclsrc":"([^"]+)"/);
    			if (le!=null && le.length==2) {
    				d.localisation = le[1];
    				dojo.cookie('onLoadWebtrendsCookie', null, { path : '/', expires : '-1' });
    			}
    		}

            // Browse Aisle, Promo Page and Search tracking
            if (dojo.query('body.browse, body.search').length>0) {
            	if (location.search.indexOf('searchTerm=')>0) {
            		d.search_term = analytics.utils.get_parameter('searchTerm');
            		d.search_term = d.search_term=='' ? analytics.utils.get_parameter('manufacturer') : d.search_term;
	                d.catalog = 'Search_' + d.search_term.replace(/\+/g, ' ').toLowerCase()+'_';
	                d.search = true;
	                d.location = 'Search';
            	} else if (location.pathname.match(/(^\/online\/(national|[a-z]{2,3}-(regional|metro)-[a-z-]+)\/promo|ColesBrowsePromotionView$)/i)) {
					d.location = 'Promotion Page';
    			} else {
            		d.aisle = [];
	                d.location = 'Aisle';
					aisle = location.pathname.match(/\/online\/[^\/]+\/([^\/]+)\/?([^\/]+)?\/?([^\/]+)?$/i);
					if (aisle!=null && aisle.length==4) {
						aisle.shift();
						for(var i=0; i<aisle.length; i++){
							if (aisle[i]==undefined)
								aisle[i]='';
							else
								d.aisle.push(aisle[i]);
						}
						d.catalog = aisle.join('_');
					} else {
						d.aisle = ['Not available'];
					}
				}
            }
            
			if (dojo.query('body.browse, body.search').length>0) {
            	if (location.pathname.match(/SearchDisplay/i) && document.referrer.match(/searchTerm=[^&]+(&|$)/i)){
					d.preceding_search = true;
					var search_success = dojo.cookie('searchSuccess');
					if (search_success == 'true'){
						d.search_result = 'success';
					}
					dojo.cookie('searchSuccess', 'false');
				}
				
				if (location.pathname.match(/SearchDisplay/i)){
					if(dojo.query('div#searchResults form').length == 0){
						d.search_result=='success' ? d.search_result = 'no_results_first_search' : d.search_result = 'no_results';
					}	
				}
            }

        	// Set product sort options
        	var sortCookie = dojo.cookie('ColesSortCookie');
        	var viewCookie = dojo.cookie('ColesSearchViewCookie');
        	var sort_option = ['Relevancy', 'A-Z (Brand)', 'A-Z (Product Name)', 'Lowest price first', 'Lowest unit price first', 'Specials first', 'Top products']; 
       		var view = viewCookie ? viewCookie : 'list';
        	
        	if (dojo.query('body.search').length > 0) {
				if (!sortCookie){	 		
					d.sort_by = d.search ? view+':'+sort_option[0] : view+':'+sort_option[6];
					
				} else {
					// Use cookie value for sort option		
					d.sort_by = view+':'+sort_option[parseInt(sortCookie)];
				}
        	}
        	
        	// Auto Suggest and Related Search
        	dojo.query('form#search').on('submit', function(){
        		sessionStorage.searchTerm = query('input#searchTerm').val();
        	});
        	dojo.query('div#search-asst a').on('click', function(){
        		sessionStorage.searchTerm = query('input#searchTerm').val();
				sessionStorage.searchMethod = 'related';
        	});
        	
        	if (d.search) {
				var typed 		= sessionStorage.searchTerm==undefined ? 'not set' : sessionStorage.searchTerm.toLowerCase();
				var entered 	= d.search_term.replace(/(\+|%20)/g, ' ').toLowerCase();
				var searched	= dojo.query('div#searchDisplay div#pageHead h1').text().replace(/(^\s+|\s+$)/g, '').toLowerCase();;

				d.search_terms 			= [searched, entered, typed];
				d.search_method			= sessionStorage.searchMethod;
				
				if (d.search_method==undefined && typed=='not set')
					d.search_method = 'promo';
				if (d.search_method==undefined && typed == entered && typed == searched)
					d.search_method = 'typed';
				if (d.search_method==undefined && typed == entered && entered != searched)
					d.search_method = 'auto-correct';
				if (d.search_method==undefined && typed != entered && entered == searched)
					d.search_method = 'auto-suggest';
			
				sessionStorage.removeItem('searchTerm');
				sessionStorage.removeItem('searchMethod');
        	}
    
            // Internal Campaign Click Tracking with handling for localisation and login
			var url_path = location.pathname.match(/(\/[^\/]+)\/?$/i);
            // if cid/WT.mt_id present then also set pid
            var ic_u = location.search.match(/(WT.ic_id|WT.mc_id|pid|cid)=([^&$]+)/i);
            if (ic_u && ic_u.length == 3){
	            if (ic_u && ic_u.length == 3){
					var date = new Date();
					date.setTime(date.getTime()+(3*60000)); // mins
					var exp = date.toGMTString(); 
					dojo.cookie('ic_id', ic_u[2]+"|"+url_path[1], {path: '/', expires: exp});
					d.int_campaign_c = ic_u[2]; 
				}
            }

            // if no ic_id on current page but cookie has ic_id then use cookie value then delete it
            var ic_c = dojo.cookie('ic_id');
            if (ic_u == null && ic_c != null && ic_c.match(url_path[1]) && location.hash!='#overlay=logIn') {
                ic_c = ic_c.split('|');
				d.int_campaign_c =  ic_c[0]; 
                dojo.cookie('ic_id', '', {path: '/', expires: -1});
            }
            
            // External Campaign Tracking using WT parameter
            var ec = location.search.match(/(WT.mc_id|cid)=([^&$]+)/i);
            if (ec != null && ec.length == 3) {
                d.ext_campaign_id = ec[2];
				if (d.int_campaign_c==undefined || d.int_campaign_c==null){
					d.int_campaign_c = d.ext_campaign_id;
				}	
            }
            // Internal Campaign Impression Tracking 
            d.int_campaign_i = [];
            query('div.espot a[href*="WT.ic_id"]').forEach(function (link) {
                var pos = d.catalog ? d.catalog : '';
                var ic = link.getAttribute('href').match(/WT.ic_id(%3d|=)([^&$]+)/i);
                if (ic != null && ic.length == 3) {
                    d.int_campaign_i.push({
                        'name': ic[2],
                        'pos': pos
                    });
                }
            });

            // Detect My Usuals page
			if (location.pathname.match(/\/AjaxAccountWishListDisplayView/i)){
            	d.my_usuals_list = true;
                d.location = location.search.indexOf('listName=My+Usuals')>0 ? 'My Usuals' : 'My Lists';
            }
            if (dojo.query('body.home').length > 0) {
            	if(dojo.query('div#my-usuals a.action-addToTrolley').length > 0){
            		d.my_usuals_home_i = true;
            	}
            }

            // Detect Product Details Page
            dojo.query('form#analytics-data-product-productdetails').forEach(function(e){
            	d.product_details = {
            		'id':   dojo.query('input[name="WT.pn_sku"]', e).val(),
            		'name': dojo.query('input[name="WT.cg_s"]',   e).val()
            	};
                d.location = 'Product Details';
            });
            
            // Detect National Home Pages
            if (location.pathname.match(/^\/online\/national(\/?$|\/info\/first-shop-free-delivery$)/i)) {
            	d.homepage = location.pathname;
                d.location = 'Homepage';
			}

            // Detect Regional Home Pages
            if (location.pathname.match(/^\/online\/[a-z]{2,3}-(regional|metro)-[a-z-]+(\/?$|\/\?)/i)) {
                d.location = 'Homepage';
			}

            // Detect My Orders page        
            if (location.pathname.match(/\/AjaxOrderDetail/i)){
            	d.my_orders = true;
				d.location = 'My Orders';
            }
            
			// Product Tracking
			var position = 0;
			var products = {};
			var selector = [
				'div.prodtile > form',
 				'div.product-box > form'
			];
			dojo.query(selector.join(', ')).forEach(function(item){
				position++;
				var placement = item.id.replace(/_?catEntryForm_\d+$/, '').replace(/_/g, '-');
				dojo.query('span.marketedEspotDescription', item).forEach(function(element){placement='PREMIUM_ESPOT';});
				if (d.product_details){
					placement = placement=='' ? 'PRODUCT_DETAILS' : placement;
					d.int_campaign_c = d.int_campaign_c ? d.int_campaign_c.replace(/_\d+$/i, '') : '';
				}
				if (d.my_usuals_list || d.my_usuals_home_i){
					placement = placement=='' ? (d.my_usuals_list ? 'List' : 'My-Usuals') : placement;
					d.catalog = d.my_usuals_home_i ? 'Home-Page' : 'My-Lists';
				}	
				var promotion = ((placement=='PRODUCT_DETAILS' || placement=='') && !d.int_campaign_c && !d.search) ? false : true;
				if (placement=='')
					placement = 'List';
				var p_category = (d.catalog || (d.product_details ? '' : 'Home-Page'))+'|'+placement;
				d.placement = placement;
				d.category = p_category;
                dojo.query('div[data-refresh]', item).forEach(function (node) {
					if (node.getAttribute('data-refresh').match(/partNumber:\s+"(\d+)/m).length==2) {
						var p_sku 			= node.getAttribute('data-refresh').match(/partNumber:\s+"(\d+)/m)[1];
						var cat_entry_id 	= 'catEntry_' + node.getAttribute('data-refresh').match(/catEntryId:\s+"(\d+)/m)[1];
						var links 			= dojo.query('div.detail a.product-url', node);
						var class_name		= node.className;
						promotion = (class_name && class_name.match(/promo/)) ? true : promotion;
						links = (links.length != 0) ? links : dojo.query('div.productTitle a.accessibility', node)
						var p_name 			= links[0].href.match(/[^$\/]+$/);
						if (products[cat_entry_id]==null) {
							products[cat_entry_id] = {
								location: 		d.location,
								feature_spot: 	placement,
								term_aisle:		d.aisle ? d.aisle.join('_') : (d.search_terms ? d.search_terms[0] : ''),
								category: 		p_category,
								sku: 			p_sku,
								name: 			p_name[0],
								promotion: 		promotion,
								position: 		position,
								s_type: 		class_name
							};	
						}
					}
                });
			});
			if (location.pathname.match(/COLForgottenNConsiderItemsView$/))
				products = {};
				
			if (d.my_orders){
				products = {};
				analytics.utils.my_order_list(products, d);
			}	
				
			d.products = [products];
				
            // Detect Login event
            query('input[name="WT.z_signon"], div#myOffersElement[data-refresh*="justLoggedIn"]').forEach(function (e) {
				if ((e.name=='WT.z_signon' && document.referrer=='') || (e.id=='myOffersElement'))
	                d.login_event = 'from_ribbon';
            });

			// Set UserID
			var user_id = document.cookie.match(/WC_USERACTIVITY_([^=]+)/);
			if (user_id != null && user_id.length==2 && user_id[1]>0 && query('div.contact > a[title="Log out"]').length>0)
				d.user_id = user_id[1]; 

            // Detect Registration
            query('input[name="WT.z_regmeth"]').forEach(function (e) {
                d.registration_event = (e.value == 'register' ? 'from_ribbon' : 'from_checkout');
            });
            
            // Detect DSS Page
            if (location.pathname.match(/\/COLDeliverySlotSelectorView$/i)) {
            	d.dss_viewed = 'Ribbon';
				var r = query('div.hd-slots-wrapper div.dss-restricted-items-slots div.times-slot');
				if (r.length>0) {
					d.restriction = r[0].getAttribute('data-time-slots').match(/slotRestriction: '([^']+)'/)[1];
				}            	
            }

			// Set section and categories
			d.section = [];
			if (d.homepage || query('body.guest, body.home').length>0) 
				d.section.push('home');
			if (d.aisle)
				d.section = d.section.concat(d.aisle);
			if (query('body.search').length>0) {
				if (d.search)
					d.section.push('search');
				else
					d.section.push('browse:facets');
			}
			if (query('body.member').length>0) {
				d.section.push('member');
				d.section.push(query('ul.breadcrumb li:nth-child(2)').text().replace(/(^\s|\s+→$)/g, '').replace(/\s/g, '-').toLowerCase());
			}
			if (query('body.content').length>0) {
				if (query('body.logOff').length>0) {
					d.section.push('logout');
				} else {
					d.section.push('content');
					d.section.push(query('ul.breadcrumb li:nth-child(2)').text().replace(/(^\s|\s+→$)/g, '').replace(/\s/g, '-').toLowerCase());
				}
			}

            // Localisation Data
            d.cust = 'personal';
            var x, l = dojo.cookie('analyticsCookie');
			if (l != undefined) {
				x = l.split('|');
				for (var i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
					d[x[i].match(/WT.z_([^:]+):/)[1]] = x[i].match(/([^:$]+)$/)[1];
				}
			}

			// Order History Count
			var clv = dojo.cookie('analytics_clv');
			if (clv) {
				var clv_a = clv.split(';');
				if (clv_a.length==1 && d.login_event) {
					d.cl = 'New';
					clv = '0;0';
				}
				dojo.cookie('analytics_clv', clv, {path: '/', expires: 365});
			} else {
				d.cl = 'New';
				dojo.cookie('analytics_clv', '0', {path: '/', expires: 365});
			}
			
			// check if spend stretch banner appears
			if(dojo.query('div#myOffersElement ul#youroffers a').length > 0){
				d.offer = 'Offer Seen';
			}

            // Detect My Usuals page add to cart event
            if (dojo.query('body.home').length > 0) {
            	query('div#my-usuals a.action-addToTrolley').on('click', function (e) {
	            	d.my_usuals_home_c = true;
            	});
            }
            
            // Detect Order on My Orders page
            if (dojo.query('body.home div#my-previous ul.displayList li').length > 1 || dojo.query('body.member table.orderTable').length > 1) {
            	d.cl = 'Experienced';
            }
            
        },
        handlers: function (d, query, topic) {
            query('div#myAccount > button.action-register').on('click', function () {
                analytics.track({
                    'page': '/virtual/registration/open_registration_form'
                });
            });
            
            // Internal campaign tracking for localisation links
            query('div.espot a.action-localise[href*="WT.ic_id"]').on('click', function (e) {
				if (this.href) {
					var ic = this.href.match(/WT.ic_id=([^&$]+)/i);
					var args = {};
					if (ic != null && ic.length == 2) {
						args['int_campaign_c'] =  ic[1]; 
						analytics.track(args);
					}
				}
            });        

            // Detect ajax request completions
            topic.subscribe('wcs/ajax/success', function (a, b) {
                var args = {user_id: d.user_id};
                analytics.log('wcs/ajax/success: ' + a.context);
                switch (a.context) {
					case 'productElement.trolleyAdd':
						if (location.pathname.match(/COLForgottenNConsiderItemsView$/))
							break;
						args.event = 'add-to-cart';
						if (d.int_campaign_c)
							args['int_campaign_c'] = d.int_campaign_c;

						if (d.catalog) {
							var rank = parseInt(query('div[data-catentry^="catEntry_"]').indexOf(query('div[data-catentry="' + a.divId + '"]')[0]) + 1);
							if (rank) {
								args['rank'] = rank;
								args['catalog'] = d.catalog;
								if (d.page_offset) args['rank'] += d.page_offset;
							}
						}
						if (d.products[0][a.divId]) {
							args.promo = d.products[0][a.divId];
						}

						if (d.aisle)
							args.aisle = d.aisle;
						if (d.product_details)
							args.product_details = true;
						if (d.search) {
							args.search = true;
							args.search_terms = d.search_terms;
							dojo.cookie('searchSuccess', 'true');
							args.search_result = 'success';
						}	
						if (d.my_usuals_home_c) {
							args.my_usuals = true;
							d.my_usuals_home_c = false;
						}
						if (d.my_usuals_list)
							args.my_usuals = true;
						if (d.my_orders)
							args.my_orders = true;
						var i=0; for (x in args){i++};		
						if (i>1)
							analytics.track(args);
						break;
					
					case 'wcs.header.search':
						sessionStorage.searchTerm = a.term;
						break;
						
	                case 'overlay.initialize':
						if (a.id=='multiSKUPromotionOverlay') {
							args.promos = {};
							require(['dojo/dom-construct'], function(dc) {
								var response_dom = dc.toDom(b);
								args.promos = analytics.utils.special_case(response_dom, args, d);
							});
							var has_object=0; for (x in args.promos){has_object++};		
							if (has_object>1){
								d.products.unshift(args.promos);
								analytics.track(d);
							}
						}
						break;
						
					case 'refreshController.refreshArea':
						switch (a.serviceId) {
						case 'ColesCategoryView':
						case 'ColesSearchView':
							d['page_offset'] = parseInt(a.beginIndex)+query('div.genericESpot div.prodtile').length;
							
							args.promos = {};
							require(['dojo/dom-construct'], function(dc) {
								var response_dom = dc.toDom(b);
								args.promos = analytics.utils.special_case(response_dom, args, d);
							});
							var has_object=0; for (x in args.promos){has_object++};		
							if (has_object>1){
								d.products = [args.promos];
								analytics.track(d);
							}
							break;
						}
						break;

	                case 'memberOrder.cancelOrder':
	                case 'memberOrder.modifyOrder.addItem':
               		case 'memberOrder.modifyOrder.changeTime':
               		case 'memberOrder.modifyOrder.changeFulfilment':
               		case 'memberOrder.modifyOrder.changePayment':
	                	var last_order = analytics.utils.order.get(a.orderId);
	                	last_order = last_order ? last_order : {order: {id: a.orderId, mod_count: 0}};
	                	args.refund = last_order.order.id+'-'+last_order.order.mod_count;
						++last_order.order.mod_count;
	                	args.order  = last_order.order;
	                	switch (a.context) {
	                		case 'memberOrder.cancelOrder':
	                			args['operation'] = 'Cancelled';
	                			args['reason'] = '';
								break;

	                		case 'memberOrder.modifyOrder.addItem':
	                			args['operation'] = 'Modified';
	                			args['reason'] = 'Add Items';
								break;

	                		case 'memberOrder.modifyOrder.changeTime':
	                			args['operation'] = 'Modified';
	                			args['reason'] = 'Change Delivery Time';
								break;

	                		case 'memberOrder.modifyOrder.changeFulfilment':
	                			args['operation'] = 'Modified';
	                			args['reason'] = 'Change Fulfilment';
								break;

	                		case 'memberOrder.modifyOrder.changePayment':
	                			args['operation'] = 'Modified';
	                			args['reason'] = 'Change Payment Method';
								break;
	                	}
						if (args.operation=='Modified') 
							analytics.utils.order.set(last_order.order.id, last_order.order);
						else
							analytics.utils.order.remove(last_order.order.id);
						analytics.track(args);
						break;						
                }
            });
            
            topic.subscribe('wcs/ajax/end', function (a, b) {
        		if (a=="overlay.initialize"){
					dojo.query('a.popup-close, div.popup-mask-closable').on('click', function(){
						d.products.shift();
					});
            	}
            });
        },
        init: function (d) {
			(function(i,s,o,g,r,a,m){i['GoogleAnalyticsObject']=r;i[r]=i[r]||function(){
			(i[r].q=i[r].q||[]).push(arguments)},i[r].l=1*new Date();a=s.createElement(o),
			m=s.getElementsByTagName(o)[0];a.async=1;a.src=g;m.parentNode.insertBefore(a,m)
			})(window,document,'script','//www.google-analytics.com/analytics.js','ga');

			// Override push method on dataLayer Array so we can process event data being added to the dataLayer
			window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
			window.dataLayer.push = function(){
				var result = Array.prototype.push.apply(this,arguments);
				if (result>0 && arguments!=undefined && arguments.length>0 && arguments[0].event) {
					analytics.log('Event pushed to dataLayer');
					var d = analytics.d, a;
					while (window.dataLayer!=undefined && window.dataLayer.length>0) {
						a = window.dataLayer.shift();
						for (var p in a) {
							d[p] = a[p];
						}
					}
					try {
						analytics.d = d;
						analytics.log('DataLayer:', d);
						if (d.event && d.event.match(/add-to-trolley|page_load|onclicking_Tab/))
							d = analytics.utils.clean_upsell_dl(d);
						analytics.track(d);
					} catch (e) {
						analytics.log(e);
						analytics.ga({
							'exception': e.message
						});
					}
				}
				return result;
			}

// 			require(["dojo/io/script"], function(script){
// 				var deferred = script.get({'url': '//si.process180.com/js/surveyinitiator.pack.js'});
// 				deferred.then(function(){analytics.si(d)});
// 			});

            require(['dojo/query', 'dojo/topic', 'dojo/io/script', 'dojo/domReady!'], function (query, topic, script) {

                try {
					analytics.aa_loaded = script.get({'url': '/wcsstore/ColesStorefrontAssetStore/mobile20/src/libs/adobe_analytics.js'});
                    analytics.handlers(d, query, topic)
                    analytics.rules(d, query, topic);
                    analytics.track(d);
                } catch (e) {
                    analytics.log(e);
                    analytics.ga({
                        'exception': e.message
                    });
                }
            });
        }
    };
    if (active)
        analytics.init(analytics.d);

})(true); // Catalogue version 2.14

</script>
            </div>

function getQueryVariable(variable) {
       var query = window.location.search;
       var vars = query.split("&");
       for (var i=0;i<vars.length;i++) {
       var pair = vars[i].split("=");
if (pair[0] === variable) {
var sast = pair[1];
switch (sast.toLowerCase()) {
case 'bread':
breadSA();
break;
case 'chocolate':
chocSA();
break;
case 'gluten+free':
glutenFreeSA();
break;
case 'organic':
organicSA();
break;
case 'coffee':
coffeeSA();
break;
case 'beer':
beerSA();
break;
case 'wine':
wineSA();
break;
case 'coffee+pods':
case 'coffee+capsules':
coffeePodSA();
break;
case 'chips':
chipsSA();
break;
case 'white+wine':
whiteWineSA();
break;
case 'red+wine':
redWineSA();
break;
}
}
}
}

if(window.location.href.indexOf("searchTerm") > -1 && window.location.href.indexOf("multiSearch") < 0) {
getQueryVariable('searchTerm');
}


</script>

function getQueryVariable2(variable) {
       var query = window.location.search;
       var vars = query.split("&");
       for (var i=0;i<vars.length;i++) {
       var pair = vars[i].split("=");
if (pair[0] === variable) { 
return pair[1];
}
}
};
